    Introduction

    API RESTFul para o gerenciamento de pedidos de um E-commerce utilizando o framework Laravel, cont√™m os m√≥dulos Comprador, Produto, Checkout, Auth e Usu√°rio

    API RESTFul E-commerce

    Base URL

    https://localhost

    Authenticating requests

    Authenticate requests to this API's endpoints by sending an Authorization header with the value "Bearer {ACCESS_TOKEN}".

    All authenticated endpoints are marked with a requires authentication badge in the documentation below.

    Voc√™ pode recuperar um token clicando em Gerar API token.

    Autentica√ß√£o Jwt

    Autentica√ß√£o com email e senha

    Obtenha um JWT com credenciais fornecidas

    Example request:
    curl --request POST \
    "https://localhost/api/auth/login" \
    --header "Content-Type: application/json" \
    --header "Accept: application/json" \
    --data "{
    \"email\": \"danielfalcao.df@gmail.com\",
    \"password\": \"123456\"
}"

    $client = new \GuzzleHttp\Client();
$response = $client->post(
    'https://localhost/api/auth/login',
    [
        'headers' => [
            'Accept' => 'application/json',
        ],
        'json' => [
            'email' => 'danielfalcao.df@gmail.com',
            'password' => '123456',
        ],
    ]
);
$body = $response->getBody();
print_r(json_decode((string) $body));
    const url = new URL(
    "https://localhost/api/auth/login"
);

const headers = {
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
    "Accept": "application/json",
};

let body = {
    "email": "danielfalcao.df@gmail.com",
    "password": "123456"
}

fetch(url, {
    method: "POST",
    headers,
    body: JSON.stringify(body),
}).then(response => response.json());
    import requests
import json

url = 'https://localhost/api/auth/login'
payload = {
    "email": "danielfalcao.df@gmail.com",
    "password": "123456"
}
headers = {
  'Content-Type': 'application/json',
  'Accept': 'application/json'
}

response = requests.request('POST', url, headers=headers, json=payload)
response.json()

    Request      

    POST api/auth/login

    Body Parameters

    email  string  

    Email do usu√°rio cadastrado.

    password  string  

    Senha do usu√°rio cadastrado.

    Cadastrar um novo usu√°rio

    Usando name, email, password e password_confirmation, se tudo estiver certo apresenta um token de acesso (JWT) e datalhes do usuario novo

    Example request:
    curl --request POST \
    "https://localhost/api/auth/register" \
    --header "Content-Type: application/json" \
    --header "Accept: application/json" \
    --data "{
    \"name\": \"teste\",
    \"email\": \"teste@teste.com\",
    \"password\": \"123456\",
    \"password_confirmation\": \"123456\"
}"

    $client = new \GuzzleHttp\Client();
$response = $client->post(
    'https://localhost/api/auth/register',
    [
        'headers' => [
            'Accept' => 'application/json',
        ],
        'json' => [
            'name' => 'teste',
            'email' => 'teste@teste.com',
            'password' => '123456',
            'password_confirmation' => '123456',
        ],
    ]
);
$body = $response->getBody();
print_r(json_decode((string) $body));
    const url = new URL(
    "https://localhost/api/auth/register"
);

const headers = {
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
    "Accept": "application/json",
};

let body = {
    "name": "teste",

    Deslogar da Api

    requires authentication

    Desconecte o usu√°rio (invalide o token), se tudo estiver certo apresenta as informa√ß√µes do usu√°rio

    Example request:
    curl --request POST \
    "https://localhost/api/auth/logout" \
    --header "Authorization: Bearer {ACCESS_TOKEN}" \
    --header "Content-Type: application/json" \
    --header "Accept: application/json"
    $client = new \GuzzleHttp\Client();
$response = $client->post(
    'https://localhost/api/auth/logout',
    [
        'headers' => [
            'Authorization' => 'Bearer {ACCESS_TOKEN}',
            'Accept' => 'application/json',
        ],
    ]
);
$body = $response->getBody();
print_r(json_decode((string) $body));
    const url = new URL(
    "https://localhost/api/auth/logout"
);

const headers = {
    "Authorization": "Bearer {ACCESS_TOKEN}",
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
    "Accept": "application/json",
};

fetch(url, {
    method: "POST",
    headers,
}).then(response => response.json());
    import requests
import json

url = 'https://localhost/api/auth/logout'
headers = {
  'Authorization': 'Bearer {ACCESS_TOKEN}',
  'Content-Type': 'application/json',
  'Accept': 'application/json'
}

response = requests.request('POST', url, headers=headers)
response.json()

    Compradores

    Buscar todos Compradores

    requires authentication

    Apresenta uma lista de todos os compradores com as informa√ß√µes

    Example request:
    curl --request GET \
    --get "https://localhost/api/buyers" \
    --header "Authorization: Bearer {ACCESS_TOKEN}" \
    --header "Content-Type: application/json" \
    --header "Accept: application/json"
    $client = new \GuzzleHttp\Client();
$response = $client->get(
    'https://localhost/api/buyers',
    [
        'headers' => [
            'Authorization' => 'Bearer {ACCESS_TOKEN}',
            'Accept' => 'application/json',
        ],
    ]
);
$body = $response->getBody();
print_r(json_decode((string) $body));
    const url = new URL(
    "https://localhost/api/buyers"
);

const headers = {
    "Authorization": "Bearer {ACCESS_TOKEN}",
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
    "Accept": "application/json",
};

fetch(url, {
    method: "GET",
    headers,
}).then(response => response.json());
    import requests
import json

url = 'https://localhost/api/buyers'
headers = {
  'Authorization': 'Bearer {ACCESS_TOKEN}',
  'Content-Type': 'application/json',
  'Accept': 'application/json'
}

response = requests.request('GET', url, headers=headers)
response.json()

    'https://localhost/api/products/delete/19',
    [
        'headers' => [
            'Authorization' => 'Bearer {ACCESS_TOKEN}',
            'Accept' => 'application/json',
        ],
    ]
);
$body = $response->getBody();
print_r(json_decode((string) $body));
    const url = new URL(
    "https://localhost/api/products/delete/19"
);

const headers = {
    "Authorization": "Bearer {ACCESS_TOKEN}",
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
    "Accept": "application/json",
};

fetch(url, {
    method: "DELETE",
    headers,
}).then(response => response.json());
    import requests
import json

url = 'https://localhost/api/products/delete/19'
headers = {
  'Authorization': 'Bearer {ACCESS_TOKEN}',
  'Content-Type': 'application/json',
  'Accept': 'application/json'
}

response = requests.request('DELETE', url, headers=headers)
response.json()

    import requests
import json

url = 'https://localhost/api/users/me/edit'

    "name": "incidunt",
    "email": "omnis"
}

  'Authorization': 'Bearer {ACCESS_TOKEN}',
  'Content-Type': 'application/json',
  'Accept': 'application/json'
}
